## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Rust Borrow Checker MIR Analysis Chain

## Your Task

Trace how the Rust borrow checker analyzes MIR (Mid-level IR) in rust-lang/rust. Find Rust source files implementing: the MIR borrow check entry point, the place conflict detection, the live range calculation, and the two-phase borrow resolution.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## MIR Borrow Checker Analysis Chain

### 1. Entry Point (`compiler/rustc_borrowck/src/lib.rs`)
- **`mir_borrowck`** — the main query registered via `provide()`. Creates a `BorrowCheckRootCtxt` and calls `do_mir_borrowck()`
- **`borrowck_collect_region_constraints`** — clones MIR, introduces NLL region variables, builds `BorrowSet`, runs MIR type-checker
- **`borrowck_check_region_constraints`** — solves region constraints and performs the final borrow-checking walk

### 2. Place Conflict Detection (`compiler/rustc_borrowck/src/places_conflict.rs`)
- **`places_conflict`** — public helper for checking place conflicts
- **`borrow_conflicts_with_place`** — core conflict check given borrow kind and access depth
- **`place_components_conflict`** — iterates projection elements in lockstep to detect overlap
- **`place_projection_conflict`** — compares individual projection elements (Deref, Field, Index, etc.)
- **`PlaceConflictBias`** — controls how unknown index comparisons are treated

### 3. Live Range Calculation (multiple files)
- **`liveness::generate`** (`type_check/liveness/mod.rs`) — main entry, partitions locals into relevant vs. boring
- **`trace::trace`** (`type_check/liveness/trace.rs`) — heart of liveness: reverse DFS from uses to definitions
- **`LocalUseMap`** (`type_check/liveness/local_use_map.rs`) — maps locals to their def/use/drop locations
- **`LivenessValues`** (`region_infer/values.rs`) — stores CFG points where each region is live
- **`MaybeLiveLocals`** (`rustc_mir_dataflow/src/impls/liveness.rs`) — backward live-variable dataflow analysis

### 4. Two-Phase Borrow Resolution (`borrow_set.rs`, `path_utils.rs`, `lib.rs`)
- **`TwoPhaseActivation`** / **`Borrow
